The Sichuan Fellow Countrymen's Association Sends a Letter to the Drought Disaster Association to Effectively Distribute Relief Funds

The Sichuan Fellow Countrymen's Association in Shanghai sent a letter to the Shanghai Drought Relief Association stating, "Yesterday, I read in the newspaper that your association has allocated relief funds according to the severity of the disaster in various places. Our province has also received 50,000 yuan. After reading this, I dare to represent the disaster victims in Sichuan in thanking you. However, it is difficult to raise funds, and it is even more difficult to distribute them. Therefore, I have to make some suggestions to your association. Our province's disasters include natural disasters and bandit disasters. Natural disasters are droughts and floods that occur from time to time, and the disaster areas cover various regions, and the disaster is extremely severe, and it is even more difficult to investigate in detail. Bandit disasters are the scourge of the Communist bandits. It has been found that the area ravaged by the Communist bandits is more than ten counties, and the disaster victims are nearly 100,000. Even those who have escaped alone and are gathered, waiting to be fed, are also hundreds of thousands. Regardless of natural disasters or bandit disasters, in this time of hunger and cold, the hope of relief is extremely urgent. Therefore, I deeply hope that this relief fund can be distributed quickly to benefit the disaster victims. Please pay attention to how this relief fund can be effectively distributed to the hands of the victims in order to conform to the original intention of philanthropists to contribute to save people. Your Excellency, I am sure that you are also thinking about this. I respectfully submit my humble opinion and hope that you will review it. I wish you peace. The Sichuan Fellow Countrymen's Association."

Joint Meeting of Five Exchange Brokers Convened Yesterday

Unanimous Appeal to Petition for the Abolition of the Transaction Tax

Since the Ministry of Finance submitted a proposal to the Executive and Legislative Yuans to levy a transaction tax, news has spread, and various exchanges and brokerage associations in this city believe that in this time of economic depression and industrial decline, the operation of the exchanges is also sluggish. Maintaining the status quo is already difficult, and if taxes are paid again, the future of the business will be even more unimaginable. The true difficulties have been presented to the government authorities, requesting the abolition of the original proposal. It is now heard that the transaction tax case will soon be submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review and implementation. The brokerage associations of various exchanges convened a joint emergency meeting of representatives of various associations at the Yizhixiang Restaurant yesterday to discuss remedial measures. The representatives included Wang Zhengru, Wu Limen from the Securities Exchange Association, Zhan Liansheng, Wang Yingchang, Wang Jiafu, Gao Qiumei, Zhang Zhusun from the Gold Exchange Association, Zhang Weiyun, Zhu Jiansheng, Xia Rongchang, Wang Zhongliang, Yang Jingcheng from the Flour Exchange Association, Chuan Changyu, Xue Chengzhang, Xu Jianqi from the Grain Exchange Association, Bian Futang, Wu Xunqing, Shao Wenyao, Zhang Bojin, Kuang Jian from the Gauze Exchange Association, and more than twenty others. First, Chairman Bian Futang reported on the process of the chairmen of various exchanges petitioning for the cancellation of the transaction tax, the latest news from the government on the case, and a detailed description of the current difficult operating conditions of the brokers. Then, the representatives present at the meeting all agreed that if the government implements the transaction tax in this severe economic downturn, the clients will be unable to bear it, and the brokers' business will inevitably fall into an irreversible predicament. At the same time, the industrial, commercial and financial sectors will suffer huge losses by losing this trading mechanism. It is hoped that the government will consider the overall situation, understand the difficulties of the merchants, and abolish the original proposal in order to maintain the status quo. It was unanimously passed by the whole body, and it was resolved that when necessary, the various associations would send representatives to accompany the chairmen of the various exchanges to Beijing to petition, and would not stop until the goal was achieved.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits a Petition to the Municipal Government to Admonish and Detain Pawnbrokers

It Is Necessary to Investigate the Origins of Pledged Items Detained by Pawnbrokers

Explicitly Acknowledged in the Court's Decision of Non-Prosecution

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a petition to the Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of petitioning, on the 10th of this month, we received a letter from the Pawnbrokers Association stating that Wan Yuan Pawnshop on Baoshan Road, a member of the association, reported that at around 11:00 AM on November 20th of last year, the police from the North Railway Station Branch of the Public Security Bureau came to the shop to summon Xiao Xueyong, the manager of the shop, saying that a Mr. Li had reported to the bureau accusing the shop manager of concealing stolen goods for profit. They immediately went to the station to await interrogation. It was said that the reporting person, Li Tingzhang, a former patrol officer of the bureau, had a theft on November 15th, and issued a loss report on the 17th, accompanied by detectives to investigate various pawnshops without success. Later, they received a letter from the thief with two pawn tickets, which were found to be pawned at our shop. Therefore, they filed a complaint accusing our shop of concealing stolen goods for profit, etc. The shop manager saw that the clothing names and quantities on the pawn tickets were mostly inconsistent, and the most important sable-lined satin female robe on the loss report was not pawned at our shop. The rest were ordinary clothes that were difficult to distinguish. Before any explanation could be given, the personnel of the branch bureau forcibly detained him in the detention center, imprisoning him for three hours before being interrogated. The shop manager explained the errors in the case, the difficulty in identifying the facts, and the lack of intent to conceal the stolen goods. However, the interrogator of the branch bureau turned a deaf ear and ignored everything, as if they had already made up their mind. The shop manager requested that the original pawn records be retrieved for verification, and that the person who handled the pawning be brought in for questioning to clarify the facts, but was refused. All opportunities for evidence that criminal suspects should have were strictly blocked, and they were arbitrarily ordered to return to the pawnshop. The shop was extremely anxious due to the manager's detention and repeatedly requested bail pending trial, but all were rejected. On the evening of that day, the branch bureau escorted the shop manager to the Zhabei Branch of the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau, and then presented him to the General Bureau, which repeatedly transferred him, as if he were a serious criminal. It was not until the 22nd that the General Bureau approved bail. In total, the detention time lasted as long as forty-eight hours. He was yelled at and scolded, and suffered humiliation everywhere. The damage to his spirit cannot be overstated, etc., and arrived at the meeting. While verifying the matter, we received another letter from the shop stating that the case of the manager of our shop, Xiao Xueyong, being falsely accused of concealing stolen goods for profit by Li Tingzhang and being unjustly detained by the Public Security Bureau had been reported. The case has now been transferred by the Municipal Public Security Bureau to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office for investigation, and on December 28, 23rd year of the Republic, the court sent a decision of non-prosecution, declaring non-prosecution. It is very clear that our shop is not guilty. However, our shop was disturbed for no reason in its business, which is related to the future business of the industry. Therefore, we enclose a copy of the decision of non-prosecution and request verification and approval for handling. Enclosed is a copy of the decision of non-prosecution by the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office, etc., and arrived at the meeting. Based on this, we found that our pawnbroker industry, mistakenly receiving stolen goods, according to Article 17 of the Pawnbroker Business Regulations promulgated by the Bureau of Social Affairs, should be reported by the victim to the authorities at the time and receive a stamped certificate, which can be used to redeem the goods at the pawnshop without paying interest, etc., and the Bureau of Social Affairs has also issued a public notice in conjunction with the Public Security Bureau. Therefore, the method of handling this case by the North Railway Station Branch is indeed inappropriate. If this trend starts, and others follow suit, the pawnbroker industry will be in danger, and they will inevitably stop business together, which concerns the economy of the poor in society and the reputation of merchants. Therefore, we report the situation and request the Council to verify it and ask the Public Security Bureau to order its subordinates to be cautious when handling public cases in the future, and not to detain legitimate merchants with fixed business premises indiscriminately. We also request that it be forwarded to the Municipal Government for an order of protection to ensure commercial security and alleviate suffering, which would be in the public interest, etc., and arrived at the meeting. Business is a lending nature, and there is originally no intention to own it for oneself or a third party. There is no need to investigate the origins of pledged items. This is explicitly acknowledged in the decision of non-prosecution by the Shanghai Local Court, which is a fair and reasonable argument. Therefore, the Shanghai Pawnbroker Business Regulations only stipulate interest-free redemption for pawnshops that mistakenly receive stolen goods, which is consistent with the intention of the decision of non-prosecution. The North Railway Station Branch of the Public Security Bureau, in the case of Wan Yuan Pawnshop mistakenly receiving stolen goods, regarded it as knowingly buying stolen goods and applied criminal investigation procedures, which was close to rash. Moreover, since the pawnshop has a fixed business premise, there is no concern that it would falsely escape. However, the shop manager was arbitrarily detained for as long as forty-eight hours, which is contrary to the principle of protecting human rights. According to the previous situation, it is reasonable to submit a petition to your government for verification and approval, and to issue an order of protection so that legitimate merchants will not be harmed outside the law, which would be in the public interest.

The Municipal Land Bureau Announces Simplified Procedures for Surveying and Exchanging Certificates

The Municipal Land Bureau has an original planned procedure for surveying all the land in the city. Citizens often request surveying before the announcement of certificate exchange. The bureau is very concerned about the possibility of fraudulent occupation when handling applications for surveying from individual households in advance. Therefore, the handling is more cautious. According to custom, the owner must submit a petition stating the reasons for the survey and submit a single chain of deeds. After verifying that the single chain matches, a date is set for surveying. Citizens are unaware of the cumbersome procedures and misunderstand that the bureau is slow in handling matters, which is prone to misunderstandings. In order to facilitate the citizens, the bureau has specially drafted simplified procedures for handling owner's applications for surveying and certificate exchange, which have been submitted to the municipal government for record. The original text is now recorded below: Simplified procedures for the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau to handle owner's applications for surveying and certificate exchange: (1) When an owner applies for surveying and certificate exchange, they should send the field slip, grain chain, deed, or other evidence of property rights to the registration section of the fourth section of the bureau to obtain a receipt. If the slip is lost, a guarantee should be filled out and sent to the bureau for record together with three kinds of newspapers (Min Bao and Morning Post, Shen Bao or News) that published the lost slip advertisement. (2) After the owner obtains the receipt, they should present the receipt to the land clearing room of the third section, explain the reason for the survey, fill in the area, location and detailed address of the land, and pay the surveying fee and the land guarantee fee. (3) After the owner pays the surveying fee and other fees, they should present the receipt for verification. According to the number, a land clearing voucher will be issued, stating the surveying date and time, and arranging a waiting place. At the appointed time, the owner should come to the bureau on time, or at the waiting place, to meet the surveyor, and the bureau will notify the land guarantee to arrive at the site in advance. (4) For surveying land with a lost slip, the owner must first properly erect boundary stones. If it is found that the boundary stones have not been erected during the surveying, the surveying should be postponed until the boundary stones are erected, and the surveying fee and other fees should be paid again. (5) During the surveying, the owner should personally point out the boundaries, and after the land guarantee proves it, the land guarantee and the owner must sign on the survey book. (6) After setting the surveying date, if it rains at the appointed time and the surveying cannot be carried out, another surveying date will be set and the owner will be notified. If the owner does not arrive at the site to point out the boundaries during the surveying, the surveying fee should be paid again, and another surveying date will be set. (7) If the land to be surveyed is within the area that has already been surveyed and the certificate exchange has not yet been announced, the owner should identify the location when applying. If there is no error, the drawing will be made immediately and a notice will be issued for signature and acknowledgement. Only half of the surveying fee needs to be paid. (8) Anyone who presents the land license to the bureau and applies for separate surveying only needs to pay the surveying fee. If applying for division on the land certificate map, a division sketch should be attached, indicating the area of each plot, and half of the surveying fee must be paid. (9) If the owner's address changes after applying for surveying, they should immediately report it to the bureau. (10) If the slip and the land match for the land to be surveyed, the owner will be notified to come to the bureau to review the drawing within three months after the surveying. If the slip and the land do not match, or if there is a boundary dispute, the drawing will be made and the signature will be requested only after separate corrections are made. (11) After the owner signs and acknowledges the drawing and sends it to the bureau, the land certificate will be filled out within three months. If there is a surplus of land, the land certificate will be filled out within three months after the price is paid.

The Municipal Land Bureau Promulgates Regulations for Real Estate Mortgage Registration

Submitted to the Municipal Government for Approval and Promulgation

The Municipal Government has formulated eleven articles of the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau's Regulations for Real Estate Mortgage Registration, as follows: (Article 1) All real estate within the city, whose property rights certificates have been exchanged for land certificates, must be registered with the bureau after being mortgaged. (Article 2) Real estate mortgage registration must be done by the mortgagee and the mortgagor, who must bring the land certificate to the bureau to fill out the registration application form in person, and both parties must sign the form for the bureau to keep on file for future reference. (Article 3) After receiving the registration application form, the bureau will immediately indicate on the land certificate that the certificate is mortgaged to so-and-so, registered in volume so-and-so, page so-and-so, and the date of the endorsement, affix the official seal of the director of the bureau, and issue it to the mortgagee for safekeeping. (Article 4) Real estate mortgage registration fees are collected at a rate of one-thousandth of the mortgage price, but if the amount is less than one jiao, one jiao will still be collected, and it will be paid by the mortgagee. (Article 5) The mortgage period shall be agreed upon by the mortgagee and the mortgagor. If the mortgage is not redeemed after the registration expires, a lawsuit may be filed directly with the competent court. (Article 6) When the plaintiff requests to transfer the overdue land certificate and exchange it for a land certificate, the municipal infrastructure transfer tax certificate and various fees shall be paid according to the assessed value. (Article 7) If there is an extension after the mortgage, the mortgagee and the mortgagor must bring the land certificate to the bureau to refill the registration application form, and the bureau will add an endorsement on the land certificate for return, and the mortgagee will pay the registration fee in accordance with Article 4 of these regulations. (Article 8) If the mortgaged real estate is re-mortgaged to another person, the mortgage amount and the mortgage date shall not exceed the original mortgage amount and period. The registration procedures shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of these regulations. (Article 9) After the mortgagor redeems the mortgaged land certificate, both parties must bring the redeemed land certificate to the bureau to cancel the registration, and the bureau will issue it to the original owner for safekeeping after indicating the cancellation and affixing the seal. (Article 10) If there are any matters not covered by these regulations, they may be amended temporarily. (Article 11) These regulations shall be submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and promulgation.

Reorganization of Map and Embankment Boundaries in This City

Re-Demarcation and Determination of Boundaries in Four Districts Including South Shanghai

The scope of this city includes parts of the former Shanghai and Baoshan counties, so the names of each district, map and embankment are not uniform. Moreover, the original boundaries have either changed due to terrain, are difficult to examine due to being buried, or are mutually intertwined and extremely chaotic. In order to reorganize the map and embankment boundaries and unify the names, the original protection map and embankment numbers are abolished, and the boundaries are re-divided according to natural boundaries. The maps in each district are numbered with numbers such as one, two, three, and four, and the embankments are named in order of heaven, earth, yuan, and yellow. Each district is the beginning and end. The four districts of South Shanghai, Zhabei, Fahua, and Caojing have now been re-divided and determined after measurement. Other districts will also be re-divided and determined in order.

Due to Improved Weather Conditions Along the Routes

In recent days, heavy fog and drizzle have covered the coastal areas, and the weather has been unusually bad, which has affected both sea and air traffic. The Shanghai-Ping, Shanghai-Hankou, and Shanghai-Guangdong routes of China Aviation Corporation have been interrupted midway and delayed. According to the company's news yesterday, the accumulated fog had dissipated in the morning, and the weather was slightly better than before, and not as chaotic as the day before. The Shanghai-Hankou line, both east and west bound flights, and the Shanghai-Ping southbound flight, have all returned to normal. However, the Shanghai-Guangdong flight reportedly took off once yesterday, but returned midway due to fog.

Raising Funds to Expand the China Underwear Weaving and Dyeing Factory

Overseas Chinese All Highly Agree and Are Willing to Help Proceed

Shiye She Yun: Huang Hongjun, general manager of China Underwear Company, in view of the fact that overseas Chinese have been greatly squeezed out by various countries in recent years and are suffering greatly, in order to enable overseas Chinese to live and work in peace and contentment after returning to the country and achieve prosperity together, he intends to expand the scope of the China Underwear Weaving and Dyeing Factory he founded, giving overseas Chinese the opportunity to invest in established industries. The Shiye She reporter has learned the details and recorded them as follows:

Expansion Plan

The China Underwear Weaving and Dyeing Factory founded by Huang Jun has been operating for fifteen years. Due to Mr. Yin's proper management, the achievements are remarkable. It is now planned to add 1.4 million yuan in capital, combining the original capital of 2 million yuan, to purchase 20,000 spinning spindles and 450 looms. It has also been decided to purchase 400 mu of land in Lu Jia Bang, near Shanghai, with 100 mu as the factory base, 100 mu to build staff and worker housing, 100 mu as a special model village, and 200 mu as a superior model village.

Contacting Investment

After the above plan was formulated, Mr. Huang went to the United States in August of last year to contact overseas Chinese for investment. Building a Model Village

Therefore, it is specially stipulated that for every 10,000 yuan invested, 1.5 mu of model village land will be given to the overseas Chinese for building residential houses, so that they can live and work in peace and contentment and gather together. In addition, shareholders also have various benefits to enjoy endlessly.

The Ministry of Finance Approves That It Is Difficult to Levy a Uniform Tax on Rayon Interwoven Fabrics

Da Gong She Yun: The Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation had previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance, suggesting that a uniform tax be re-imposed on rayon interwoven fabrics in order to maintain the dying livelihood of silk merchants. Yesterday, the Ministry of Finance approved the association, saying: "The uniform tax is an ex-factory tax. There are no factories in the country that manufacture rayon. It is inconsistent with the principle of levying a uniform tax. If a uniform tax is opened only for rayon interwoven fabrics, each interwoven product must be identified, which will cause many difficulties. Moreover, weaving factories that use rayon as raw material are very scattered and not concentrated. Investigation is not easy and management is very difficult. Taking care of one thing and losing sight of another will result in more omissions than levies, which will still not help. The main reason for the failure of China's silk industry is the severance of overseas sales channels and the drop in silk prices, not entirely due to the proliferation of rayon. Currently, the tax rate on rayon is already over 60% ad valorem. The higher the tax rate, the more difficult it is to prevent smuggling. Therefore, increasing taxes will not protect the export of silk. The various points raised by the association are kept for reference."

The Cigarette Anti-Smuggling Association Revises the Touring Inspection Methods

Xin Xin She Yun: The Tax Bureau's Cigarette Anti-Smuggling Assistance Committee convened a committee meeting yesterday (12th) at the Tax Bureau on the second floor of the Jianghai Customs to discuss revising the touring inspection methods. Dong Zhongding, Shen Weiting, Wang Zongzhu, Bao Gengsheng, Tang Shi, Chen Maonan, Chen Shaoji, Chen Zhongpei, Shen Kunshan, Sun Lishan, Wu Tingsheng, Jin Gong, Jiang Yongyi, and more than ten others attended. Dong Zhongding chaired the meeting, He Fangliang recorded the meeting, and after the ceremony, the original text was revised as follows: (1) When the special inspectors and investigators of various districts are conducting touring inspections, they should all abide by these methods. (2) Touring inspections, in addition to the original designated inspection areas, may also be dispatched at any time to other provinces and regions when deemed necessary. (3) The special inspectors will be temporarily appointed by the Tax Bureau, and the number will not be fixed for the time being. The investigators will be dispatched by the Bureau or the Cigarette Anti-Smuggling Assistance Committee, taking into account the situation in each province and region, with a limit of five to ten people each for the time being. They will be responsible for touring investigations of all illegal cigarettes' manufacturing, sales, and transportation. If the affairs are complicated and insufficient distribution, they may be appropriately increased at any time. (4) When investigators are on duty, if they encounter the following circumstances, they should immediately report to the Bureau and the Assistance Committee: (A) The sale, transportation, or manufacture of iron hand-cranked cigarette machines that are absolutely prohibited. (B) Wooden hand-cranked machines that are purchased or transported privately. (C) Registered cigarette households that secretly establish brand names or sell fake products when manufacturing cigarettes. (D) Soil tobacco shredding shops that privately supply silk for cigarette making. (E) Shops in various places that illegally transport and sell tax-evading cigarettes and all raw materials for various cigarettes (cured tobacco leaves, cured tobacco silk, and handmade cigarette paper). (F) Ships, trains, and transportation companies that transport and unload all tax-evading or illegal tobacco products (tobacco leaves and tobacco silk) and various cigarette papers for customers. (G) Non-cured tobacco producing area registered curing tobacco silk shops that privately purchase cured tobacco leaves and shred them into cured tobacco silk for sale. (H) Other violations of various cigarette regulations and various methods. (5) When the special inspectors and investigators are dispatched to conduct touring investigations, they should fill in the investigation ten-day report form and submit it to the Bureau and the Assistance Committee every ten days for verification. However, each time they arrive at a place (counties and towns), they should also prepare a report stating the location and time of arrival and submit it in advance. On the one hand, they should purchase a five-cent postage stamp from the local postal agency and retrieve the stamped receipt as proof, which should be attached to the report and submitted. (6) If the Tax Bureau believes that it is necessary to order special personnel to handle the case based on the investigator's report, the special personnel should immediately go to the area and cooperate with the relevant authorities to earnestly handle the case. However, when necessary, the Tax Bureau may also dispatch personnel directly to conduct investigations at any time, depending on the circumstances. (7) When necessary, the special personnel may hire a clerk to assist with clerical work. (8) When special personnel are dispatched to handle cases in various places, if the investigator's testimony is required, the investigator should report the actual situation in detail for assessment. When necessary, they should still do their best to assist in the investigation. (9) If there are any matters not covered by these methods, the Tax Bureau may add them at any time.

Dongjiadu Ferry Workers Union Lawsuit

Union Funds Require a Meeting

Criminal Case Becomes a Civil Case

The ferry workers union at the Dongjiadu wharf in Pudong elected Zhao Agou as a standing committee member and Zhao Quanfu as the finance committee member two years ago (1933). Last year (1934), a re-election was held, and Ji Hegui was elected as standing committee member, while Zhang Linfa managed the finances. Recently, Ji Hegui sued Zhao Agou, Zhao Quanfu, and others at the Shanghai District Procuratorate for embezzlement of public funds, claiming that after the defendants left their positions, they should have handed over the union's remaining public funds of over 2,300 yuan in full, but they refused under various pretexts, intending to embezzle them. However, the defendants submitted a defense, stating that the union had been banned by the party department and was now suspended, and the funds were indeed in their custody, but a meeting of all committee members must be convened before they could be handed over, as they could not be transferred privately. Both sides held to their own accounts. After investigation by the prosecutor, a decision was made not to prosecute. Ji Hegui, dissatisfied with the decision, appealed to the Jiangsu High Court for reconsideration. The High Court rejected the appeal, stating that union funds should be handled through meetings, and if there were disputes, they should be resolved through civil court proceedings, as no criminal embezzlement had occurred. The original decision not to prosecute was deemed appropriate, and the request for reconsideration was without merit and should be rejected. Therefore, Ji Hegui hired someone to draft a petition to the District Court Mediation Tribunal, requesting mediation. A summons was issued, but the opposing party did not appear, resulting in no resolution. It is reported that Ji Hegui will hire a lawyer to file a formal lawsuit according to the law.

Salvation Association for Beggars Ready to Organize, Starting Today, Taking in Women, Children, and Beggars

From 8:00 AM to 4:00 PM

Registration, Bathing, Change of Clothes, and then Gruel

The Salvation Association for Beggars, organized by the Chinese Women's Temperance Association, is now ready to start taking in people today. From 8:00 AM to 4:00 PM daily, all women, children, and beggars can register at the association's central registration office inside the church at No. 3 Xihuade Road, east of the Waibaidu Bridge. After registration, they will bathe and change clothes in the association's bathroom, undergo a physical examination, and then be given gruel. They will then be sent to various institutions. Disabled or elderly female beggars will be sent to the Xinyu Hall for care. Female beggars under the age of 14 will be sent to the Shanghai Women and Children's Education Institute attached to the Jiangwan Temperance Association for care. Beggars will be sent to the Bihansuo, run by Wang Yiting and others, for care. It is also reported that Ms. Liu Wang Liming, the director of the association, has collected dozens of dan of gruel rice and over a hundred pieces of clothing from various charitable organizations and parties in preparation for today's intake.

Xu Ruikuan Accuses Neighbor of Abducting and Selling His Son

Xu Ruikuan, a native of Yancheng, resides in a straw hut without a number in Yuquegang, Dapu Road, Nanshi. He is in his forties and makes a living pulling a rickshaw. He married a woman surnamed Lü, and their only son, nicknamed Dayazi, is only four years old. On the afternoon of November 29th of the old calendar year, at about 4:00 PM, Dayazi was sold by Qian Zhuizi, a fellow rickshaw puller and fellow villager, and his accomplice Wang Delin, to the Chen family at No. 7, a certain street on Tongfu Road in the International Settlement, reportedly for a price of 30 yuan. After the boy Dayazi suddenly disappeared, Xu Ruikuan and his wife asked relatives and friends to search for him, but to no avail. On the afternoon of December 5th of the old calendar year, at 10:00 PM, Liu Zihong, a fellow Yancheng native residing with them, and Ma Dawu, a fellow villager residing in a straw hut east of Dapu Bridge, sent a letter to Xu Ruikuan, saying that his son Dayazi had been taken away by Qian Xiaokai (i.e., Qian Zhuizi) and that 15 yuan was needed to redeem Dayazi. Xu Ruikuan was overjoyed and immediately tried to raise the 15 yuan. The next day, he took the money to the Sanxinglou Tea Garden on Dapu Road to wait for his son to be redeemed, but waited until late at night without seeing anyone bring Dayazi back. Therefore, on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at about 4:00 PM, he found Qian Zhuizi, Liu Zihong, Ma Dawu, and others who resided with him, and went to the Rihuichiao Police Station of the West Gate Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, accusing Qian Zhuizi and the other two of colluding to kidnap his son Dayazi. Officer Zheng sent a police officer to accompany the plaintiff Xu Ruikuan to search for the fugitive Ma Dawu in the straw shed east of Dapu Bridge the night before, but was unsuccessful. Ma's wife, a Yancheng native surnamed Xia, was taken to the police station and, along with the others, was sent to the West Gate Branch for interrogation yesterday morning. The defendants Qian Zhuizi and Liu Zihong both admitted that they had taken Dayazi away and sold him for money. However, the buyer surnamed Chen had moved away, and the whereabouts of the fugitive accomplice Wang Delin and Dayazi were unknown. After hearing the confession, Chief Li determined that the case involved kidnapping and extortion, as well as the abduction and sale of human beings, separating family members. In addition to reporting the situation to the General Bureau for record-keeping, he also handed over the three men and women, including Qian Zhuizi, to the head of the Detective Squad stationed at the bureau, Shen Wenda, for a swift and thorough investigation. He also ordered the detective foreman Fang Lingen to be responsible for investigating and arresting the fugitive accomplices, and to bring them to justice at the General Bureau.

Discussion on Rickshaw Registration, Rickshaw Businessmen Hold General Meeting Today

New Rickshaws Too Heavy, Rickshaw Pullers Express Opposition

Because most rickshaw pullers opposed registration, the Special Zone Rickshaw Association held a regular meeting the night before last at 8:00 PM. Over twenty people attended, including Gu Songmao, Yin Zhiling, and Hou Shaoan. Gu Songmao chaired the meeting. As a result of the discussion, rickshaw pullers were advised to register, and a general meeting of members was scheduled for today. The association issued a notice to all rickshaw owners, stating that the office had resolved at the 66th board meeting to convene a member discussion meeting at the association's address at 2:00 PM on January 14th to discuss rickshaw registration and important cases regarding leased vehicles. Members were urged to attend on time, as the matter concerned their vital interests and should not be neglected. Furthermore, since the implementation of the 131 new rickshaws on New Year's Day, rickshaw pullers have expressed opposition because (1) the style is too luxurious, and most passengers suspect that they are privately owned or "wild chicken" chartered cars, so they dare not inquire, and business is slow; (2) the weight is too heavy, and the pulling time is longer for the same section of road, resulting in the daily business being less than half of the old rickshaws. Therefore, they are requesting the owners to continue to rent out the old rickshaws. The rickshaw owners plan to raise the issue for discussion at the general meeting.

Shanghai County to Convert Qiansan Township Road into Motor Road

The Shanghai County Government is planning to build the Beidong (Beiqiao to Chegou) and Qiansan (Qianjingmiao Ferry to Sanlintang) township roads in order to benefit the people. The county government has received a letter from Mr. Liu Jiping, a local notable, requesting that the Qiansan township road be expanded into a motor road in sections. A preliminary plan and budget have been drawn up, with the Qianhua section (from Qianliangmiao to Huajing) being built first. County Magistrate Pan convened a temporary meeting of the Construction Committee yesterday to discuss the matter. A resolution was passed to widen the section from Qianliangmiao to the Huangpu River to ten shichi, and the part to be expanded along the original route will not be compensated separately. The newly opened part where there is no original road will be compensated at a price of 70 yuan per mu, based on the land price of Beihui Road. The costs of all bridges and culverts will be raised separately by the county and the local area after the roadbed is built.

Walker Pan Deming to Return to China

Has Departed from America and is Walking to Soviet Russia

Expected to Arrive in Shanghai in Late May

The young walker Pan Deming joined the China Youth Asia Walking Group five years ago and set off from Shanghai. There were many participants at the time, but all dropped out one after another due to insufficient physical strength. By the time they reached French Annam, only Mr. Pan was left. Mr. Pan not only did not let the withdrawal of all his companions dampen his spirit, but instead was inspired to strive for the ambition of walking around the world. According to information from Mr. Huang Jingwan, an educator in Shanghai, and Mr. Zhang, a relative of Mr. Pan, after Mr. Pan arrived in the United States last autumn, the American newspapers competed to report on Mr. Pan's completion of the twenty-nine-country journey and praised him as a "Chinese hero." He has traveled through countries such as England, Germany, France, Italy, Belgium, Annam, Switzerland, and India, enduring great hardships along the way. Mr. Pan has now departed from America and is walking to Soviet Russia, returning to China via Siberia. He is expected to arrive in Shanghai in late May.

Severely Injured, Life in Danger

Xu Jinxi, a native of Yancheng, lives at No. 51, Beixingfa Li, Yangjiabang Road, Zhabei. His wife is surnamed Xu, and his father is Xu Zhaocheng, and his mother is surnamed Wang. This led to a disagreement between father and son. Afterwards, Jinxi was ashamed and angry, and suddenly had a desperate thought. He used a razor to slash his own throat, and blood flowed profusely. Xu Zhaocheng and his wife, surnamed Wang, were summoned to the police station for questioning after the incident.

Arrest of Counterfeit Currency Gangsters

Detained and Sent to the French Concession Police for Questioning

According to the Shanghai Times, a Chinese detective in the Hongkou Hui Si Police District arrested a Chinese man on Wednesday night, carrying about a thousand counterfeit banknotes of various kinds. These banknotes were hidden in the various compartments of a wide leather belt. There were about three hundred 20-franc notes, as well as several kinds of local national currency notes. The rest were 10-franc notes. The man claimed at the time that he came from Brazil, had lived in Vietnam, and had only recently come to Shanghai. He said that he had bought the banknotes from a passenger on the ship to Shanghai and did not know that they were counterfeit. However, the detective did not believe him and decided to detain him for further questioning. After three hours of interrogation, neither the Public Concession authorities nor the French Concession police authorities were willing to say much about the matter. It was learned last night that they are now pursuing the matter in order to uncover the organization that is using counterfeit currency in various places in the Far East.

Chen Jinlan, a native of Yong, nicknamed Shepi Jinlan, a murderer, was arrested by the French Concession police in his hometown in December of that year after fleeing the scene of the shooting of Chen Zhikui, the owner of Qianfengtai Candle Shop, with Zhu Quanxing, a native of Wuxi, at around 9:00 PM on April 14 of the previous year. He was brought to Shanghai and sent to the Special Court II for prosecution on charges of murder. He was sentenced to 14 years in prison. Gao Xiaoxu, the warden, was furious upon learning of this and transferred the six guards on duty, both inside and outside, Fang Yuqi and Zhou Wenjin, and the guards who were suspected of being involved in the shift change, both inside and outside, Yang Xingcun, Wang Guanghe, Han Haorui, and Yan Ling, to the Procuratorate of the Special Court II for investigation and interrogation. Vegetable Vendor Angrily Chops Adulterer

Someone Snores on the Bed

The Adulterer is Seriously Injured, the Wife is Slightly Injured

Bai Laosi, a native of Anhui, 43 years old, lives with his wife Bai Zhou (30 years old, a native of Nanjing) and their children at No. 94, Maiqi Road, French Concession. Bai makes a living by selling vegetables. He goes out at 2:00 AM every day to wholesale vegetables and returns home at 5:00 AM to sort them out before taking them to the vegetable market on Maiqi Road to sell. This has been his routine for a long time. Li Zhijia, a fellow villager of Bai who lives at No. 6, Lane 128, Ju Pules Road, is 47 years old and guards a water pavilion (i.e., manages an artesian well) at No. 159, Lane 159, Haige Road. Because he often asked Bai to buy vegetarian vegetables, he often went to Bai's house and became close to Bai's wife. Over time, the two developed a love affair. Li often took advantage of Bai's absence to sell vegetables at midnight to go to Bai's house for a secret rendezvous with Zhou, while Bai remained oblivious. At about 2:00 AM on the morning of the day before yesterday, Li again followed his usual practice and waited for Bai Laosi to go out before going to Bai's house to continue his affair with Bai's wife. At 5:00 AM, Bai returned home to sell vegetables and caught sight of Li and his wife sleeping in the same bed. He couldn't help but be consumed by jealousy. He grabbed a bamboo pole used to carry vegetables and beat Li and Zhou in bed. Because the two resisted, Bai, in a moment of desperation, grabbed a sharp knife used to sell vegetables and stabbed Li in the lower abdomen, plunging it several inches deep. He also stabbed Zhou in the right arm and right leg. Li and Zhou felt the pain and shouted for help. The second landlord reported the incident to the police station, and detective Xu Jinlong rushed to the scene, arresting Bai and taking him, along with the murder weapon and bamboo pole, to the police station. The injured were sent to Guangci Hospital for treatment. At noon that day, Bai was sent to the Criminal Court I of the Special Court II, where he was interrogated by Judge Zhang Chaozuo. The police lawyer Chen Ming presented the case, requesting a postponement until the victims recovered and requested a trial. When questioned, Bai confessed that he committed the crime because Li had an affair with his wife. The detective then reported the process of arresting the defendant, saying that Zhou's injuries were minor, while Li's injury was in the lower abdomen and was very serious, requesting a postponement. The court verified the report and approved the postponement of the trial, ordering the defendant to be detained and waiting for the court to go to the hospital to question the victim for further verification.

Pan Rongfu's Case Against Zhou Xinzong Overturned on Appeal

Zhou Xinzong Declared Not Guilty

The Civil Portion Also Dismissed

Pan Rongfu, a native of Dinghai County, Zhejiang, residing at No. 12, Fuxu Fang, Foch Road, runs the Pan Rongji Construction Factory. He previously hired lawyer Yuan Yang'an to file a complaint with the First Special Court against Zhou Xinzong, a native of Yin County who worked as a supervisor, for breach of trust and embezzlement of over 7,000 yuan. The Special Court sentenced Zhou to six months in prison and ordered him to compensate the full amount. Zhou, dissatisfied with the verdict, hired lawyers Chen Tingrui and others to appeal to the Second Branch of the High Court, arguing that the accounts received had actually been handed over to Pan Rongji, and citing the fact that Pan had admitted in another case that he had received the money, in order to prove the inappropriateness of the first instance judgment and requesting that it be overturned. The other day, presiding judge Yu Hua and judges Zhou and Wu came to the court to hear the case clearly and announced the judgment, the main text of which stated: "The portion of the original judgment concerning Zhou Xinzong's crime and punishment is revoked, Zhou Xinzong is not guilty, and the other appeals are rejected." The attached civil suit regarding embezzlement was also pronounced at the same time, and the original judgment was revoked and the lawsuit filed by the appellee Pan Rongji against Zhou Xinzong in the first instance to recover the money was dismissed. The judgment was delivered to both parties yesterday. The reasons for the criminal portion of the judgment are excerpted as follows: "The appellant Zhou Xinzong served as a supervisor for the plaintiff Pan Rongfu's construction factory, receiving 7,850 yuan from the Hwayeh Trust Company for the cost increase, and the Hwayeh Company issued a check for the same amount dated September 13 from the Zhejiang Industrial Bank to Zhou for receipt. The money was cashed in full. This is an undisputed fact. The only thing that needs to be investigated is whether Zhou transferred the check to Pan. As for the transfer between the two parties, there was no fixed method. One claimed that it had been transferred, the other claimed that it had not, and they only argued with empty words. Therefore, the suspicion of his crime cannot be proven, and the benefit should go to the defendant. Moreover, according to the testimony of witness Li Jinjun, an additional 8,200 yuan was issued on September 2 with the No. 50 receipt certificate. On September 22, a certificate for 10,000 yuan was re-issued. On the No. 51 receipt certificate, the 8,200 yuan was included in the previously received item. Pan signed and acknowledged it. If the No. 50 receipt certificate was not paid, he could not issue the No. 51 certificate. Between the issuance of the two certificates, Pan's representative, Di Atu, came, and he had informed him that 7,850 yuan had been paid for the 8,200 yuan increase, and 350 yuan had been temporarily withheld because some work had not been completed. Pan had already signed and acknowledged that the money opened on certificate No. 50 had already been received on certificate No. 51, and between September 2 and September 22, Li Jinjun clearly informed Pan's representative that the actual amount of 7,850 yuan had been issued and 350 yuan had been temporarily withheld. Therefore, before September 22, Pan already knew that the money had been issued, so he was willing to sign certificate No. 51. Referring to Pan's statement in the case of suing Hwayeh Company for arrears, it was briefly stated that 8,200 yuan had been added to the account, and the applicant had already signed and received it on Li Jinjun's receipt certificate, and it had already been concluded. Therefore, Pan's claim that Zhou received 7,850 yuan and that he was unaware of it is difficult to believe. The original judgment's evidence for Zhou Xinzong's crime of embezzlement in business is insufficient, and the appeal on that part should be considered reasonable. Based on the above conclusions, the judgment should be made in accordance with Articles 384, 379, 316, 507, and 385(1) of the Criminal Procedure Law." As for the reasons for the civil portion of the judgment, the civil suit was based on the occurrence of a criminal act. Since the criminal act had determined that Zhou Xinzong had no embezzlement, he should not be held responsible for returning the money. The original judgment ordering Zhou to return 7,850 yuan was unfounded and should be revoked.

Unidentified Male Corpse Found in Fanwangdu

Five or Six Knife Wounds

Reported to the Court for Autopsy

At 8:10 AM yesterday morning, an unidentified young male corpse who had been assassinated was suddenly discovered in a small river near the east of the Fanwangdu Railway Station in western Shanghai. There were five or six knife wounds on his head and face, with blood flowing profusely. The details are as follows:

Discovery of the Corpse

An unidentified male corpse was suddenly discovered in a small river on the east side of No. 1, the raised flag south of the Fanwangdu Railway Station in western Shanghai. The corpse was lying face up in the water. A villager passing by saw it and immediately reported it to the nearby police, who in turn reported it to the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau. Director Wang, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched patrol officers Long and Yang, along with Detective Team Leader Geng Shoubao, squad leader Cao Chuqiao, and detective Zhang Shaoming, to investigate.

Gruesome Scene of Assassination

The unidentified young male corpse was found lying face up in the river, with his head to the northwest and feet to the southeast. He had a fair and elongated face and was about twenty years old. He was wearing a white绒短衫 (dun duan shan - short jacket), with a green striped Western-style shirt underneath, and gray毛葛夾袴 (mao ge jia ku - lined trousers). Underneath the trousers, he had white绒布袴 (rong bu ku - fleece cloth pants). He was wearing酱色毛綫襪 (jiang se mao xian wa - maroon wool socks) and black套鞋 (tao xie - overshoes). He had a Western-style hairstyle. There were two knife wounds on the back of his neck, one knife wound on the top of his head, one knife wound directly below, one knife wound next to his right neck, and one knife wound on his forehead, for a total of six wounds. Later, a呢帽 (ni mao - felt hat) was found in the railway with the dead man's hair. There was a circle of blood stains in the middle of the road, suggesting that he was assassinated there and then the body was moved and dumped in the river.

Reporting the Autopsy and Apprehending the Murderer

After receiving the report, Director Wang not only reported it to the Public Security General Bureau but also ordered the local 保 (bao - neighborhood head) to report it to the local court for autopsy. He also ordered Detective Team Leader Geng Shoubao and squad leader Cao Chuqiao to closely apprehend the murderer and bring him to justice.

Mr. Zhuang already has over 100,000 words of travel notes and thousands of photos, which will be published soon. Mr. Zhuang will go to Beijing soon to report everything to the Northwest Development Association. The return trip will take at least a year and a half.

National Products Factory Association Requests the Return of National Exhibition Items

The Shanghai National Products Factory Association replied to the Jianghai Customs Superintendent yesterday, stating, "Approved letter opened, stating that the goods seized by this customs from the Xin Ningshao ship were privately carried by the ship's crew. If the price of the goods is fined one time, together with the transit tax, it can be released." After investigation, the goods seized by your customs from the Xin Ningshao ship were indeed carried by the factory representatives and were not privately carried by the ship's crew. When seized, the staff of our association stated to the customs officers that they were goods returned from the Ningbo National Products Exhibition. On that day, most of the goods returned by more than 200 people were tax-exempt and packed in boxes. Because the representatives on the ship had scattered goods, they were not packed in boxes and were carried with them, resulting in this miscalculation. Therefore, we hereby send another letter stating that we request tax-exempt return to alleviate the difficulties of merchants.

A Real Estate Commission Turns Bloody

Dai Laosi Was Slashed

Chen Ziqing Denies Conspiracy

Dai Laosi, a Danyang native who owns a Huiming Barber Shop at No. 800 Hainin Road, has been seeking buyers for the real estate of Zhou Xiangyun, the owner of Daqing Lane on Nanjing Road, who intends to sell the property for 6.5 million yuan. He hoped to earn a large commission after the transaction was completed. It was later discovered that a certain Cantonese wanted to buy the property, and Dai, realizing that his influence was limited and that he might not be able to win the trust of both the buyer and the seller, shared the intermediary task with Chen Ziqing (also known as Chen Zhiyun), a Wuxi native residing at No. 760 Tailai Lane on Hainin Road, who is currently working as a clerk for a lawyer, to make it easier to handle. Unexpectedly, after running around from early summer to late winter, the effort failed, and the hoped-for reward also vanished. The participants were frustrated and began to quarrel. At 3 p.m. on the 21st of last month, while Dai was at Chen's house, he was suddenly attacked from behind with a sharp kitchen knife due to this dispute, and his back was slashed, causing blood to flow immediately. Dai ran wounded to the nearby Huishi Patrol Room to report the incident. The head of the patrol ordered him to take off his clothes for inspection, and it was found that his shirt was half-covered in blood. He dispatched detectives to send Dai to the hospital for treatment and went to Chen's house to inquire about the cause of the incident, but the murderer had already escaped. Dai's injuries have now healed, and he has been discharged from the hospital. He claimed that there were four people at the scene of the crime: Chen Ziqing, Li Shurong from Shandong, Yuan Bingnan from Jiangbei, and Lu Zhensheng from Huzhou. He hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation against them for injury, requesting that they be interrogated and punished according to the law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui of the First Special District Court opened the trial. Only the defendant Chen Zhiyun appeared in court. The other three, Li, Yuan, and Lu, had all fled. The plaintiff, Dai Laosi, described the incident in detail, stating that the real estate transaction was a collaboration between him and Chen. Although the deal was not finalized, Chen demanded 50 yuan from him as compensation for the loss. Because he refused to pay, Chen repeatedly demanded the money. On October 1st, he even dragged him into the Hongkou Patrol Room, but he was released after the head of the patrol inquired. On December 14th, Chen sent Yuan Bingnan to summon him to a teahouse, still demanding the money. He still refused, so on the afternoon of December 21st, Chen suddenly sent Lu Zhensheng to the barbershop, falsely claiming that the real estate deal had been completed and ordering him to go to Chen's house to divide the money. Upon arrival, Chen was smoking opium in the inner room and ordered the crowd not to let him go. Yuan Bingnan tightly held his hand, and Li Shurong took Chen's kitchen knife and slashed him from behind. He ran wounded to the Huishi Patrol Room to report the incident. When the detectives arrived at Chen's house, the murderers had already fled. Li, Yuan, and Lu are all Chen's accomplices, so only Chen knows their whereabouts, but he refuses to help catch them. Chen Zhiyun claimed that Cao, the buyer, had given Dai 50 yuan during the negotiations. When he did not buy the property, Cao asked Dai to return the money. Dai repeatedly promised to return it, but repeatedly broke his promise. Cao once wanted to accuse him of fraud, but he did not succeed because he refused to testify. On the afternoon of the 21st, he was in a neighbor's house and heard them fighting in his house, so he rushed home, but it had already subsided. He did not know who the murderer was. If it was as Dai claimed, the Patrol Room would have investigated him. When Dai heard Chen's statement, he firmly denied receiving money from Cao, saying that Chen repeatedly demanded compensation for the loss, which led to the incident. Chen's wife, Shunzhu, was also questioned. Judge Liu ordered the hearing to be continued at a later date.

Brothers in Crime Partnered to Make Red Pills

The Manufacturing Facility Was on Luban Road

Many People Involved Have Been Apprehended

Wang Rusong, the chief detective, Zhang Daorong, the deputy detective, and Liu Jinrong, Shen Jinshu, Yang Ruyu, and other detectives from the Second Squad of the French Concession Patrol Room, while checking pedestrians on Vermon Road at 7 a.m. the day before yesterday, found a pedestrian, Zhou Tiansheng (28 years old, from Changshu, residing at No. 77 Huagen Road), holding a small bag that looked suspicious. Upon inspection, the bag contained 1,000 red pills. He was immediately arrested. According to Zhou's confession, he bought the pills from Xue Lianzhang, a Ningbo native in the front room on the second floor of No. 158 Ailig Road, for six yuan. The detectives then took Zhou to the address.

To Search

Xue Lianzhang (32 years old) was still sleeping soundly and had not gotten up. He was immediately arrested, and three bags of red pills, totaling 3,000 pills, were found under his pillow. According to Xue's confession, the pills came from Cao Linbao (also known as Lin Baobao, about 25 or 26 years old), a Tongzhou native who lived in the Fuxingyuan Teahouse at No. 127 Luban Road in the Chinese area. The pills were sent by Cao to be sold on his behalf. The detectives then took Zhou and Xue to the West Gate Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau to request detectives to assist in a secret search of the Fuxingyuan Teahouse at No. 127 Luban Road.

The Main Culprit Was Arrested

Cao Linbao had already left and was not apprehended, causing him to escape. Only Cao's brother, Cao Zhiyuan (27 years old, from Tongzhou), was arrested and taken to the bureau. After registering, he was brought back to the Patrol Room for questioning. According to Cao's confession, the manufacturing facility was located at No. 47 in the Dadefang in Lane 288 on Luban Road. Detective Wang and others immediately rushed to No. 47 in the Dadefang and again.

The People Involved Were Arrested

Lin Afu (28 years old, Ningbo native, residing at No. 11 Zhongheli on Luban Road) and Zhao Agen (17 years old, residing at the home of Cao Linbao in Fuxingyuan Teahouse at No. 127 Luban Road) were arrested. According to Lin's confession, he, Cao Linbao, and Cao Zhiyuan were partners, investing in opening a red pill manufacturing facility. Zhao admitted to being a partner in manufacturing the red pills. The two pointed out the manufacturing facility, located in the rear building on the third floor of No. 42 in the same lane, Dadefang. The detectives went to search and seized.

Red Pill Manufacturing Equipment

Two sets of pill-making boards, four baking ovens, one balance scale, two sieves, and two boxes of raw material powder and Taikoo sugar. The suspects and evidence were taken to the Patrol Room for investigation. Detectives were also sent to Xue Lianzhang's home at No. 158 Ailig Road to wait for and arrest accomplices. At 2 p.m., Zhang Xiaochang (18 years old), a Tongzhou native who specialized in transporting red pills, arrived and was arrested by the detective waiting there and taken to the Patrol Room. This morning, they were sent to the Second Special Court for prosecution and trial.

Jinshan County Colludes to Beat Foster Daughter to Death

Qiu Juanbao and Others Fled to Shanghai in Fear of Punishment

The Body Was Thrown into Taihu Lake and Then Floated Up

Qiu Juanbao, 35, a woman from Liujiazhen, 12 miles from the city in Jinshan County, owns farmland. Her husband, Wu Youren, 51, are both addicted to opium. They have one adopted daughter, named Yindi, who is now six years old. The stepmother disliked the adopted daughter's fate and often beat and abused her. However, there were no neighbors, and they lived alone in a house, with no one to interfere. As a result, Yindi was forbidden to cry even when she was beaten. A week ago, Juanbao lost hundreds of yuan in a mahjong game and blamed Yindi's fate, inflicting cruel torture. Unexpectedly, she was beaten to death. Because no one knew, Juanbao put Yindi's body in a burlap sack and instructed her relatives to throw it into Taihu Lake (the relative is Chen Delin, who has now been arrested and is highly suspected). Several days later, the corpse, along with the burlap sack, suddenly floated up and was recovered by a fishing boat. Only then was the girl's body discovered. The county was immediately notified for inspection and investigation. Only then was it known that she was the adopted daughter of Qiu Juanbao. They immediately went to arrest her, but Qiu Juanbao had fled to Shanghai with her entire family. After investigation by the Jinshan County Government, it was discovered that Qiu Juanbao and others were hiding at No. 26 Kaiming Lane, Ji畝地 in Shanghai. A document was specially prepared and sent to Shanghai by Zhang Zhenhua, a patrol officer from the Second Resident Station of the County Public Security Bureau, and Item Weishan, a bailiff, to the Lao Beimen Police Station under their jurisdiction, requesting the dispatch of police to assist in the arrest. Wei Kunquan, police officer No. 9, was dispatched to arrest Qiu Juanbao, Wu Youren, and Chen Delin and brought them to the station. After questioning by Director Shen, it was determined that the case involved assisting in the arrest of major criminals in a homicide case, and it was decided to send them to the General Bureau for investigation and disposition.

Female Teacher Drowns Herself

Zheng Juying, a female teacher who used to work at a certain municipal elementary school in Hangzhou, was in her twenties and from Luodian, Baoshan. In August of last year, she married Li Guozhong, a Jiashan native, through a matchmaker. The couple's love was very strong. In July of this year, she gave birth to a son. Recently, Zheng returned home due to an incident and suddenly had the idea of ending her life due to some kind of stimulation. She was spotted by a pedestrian there, who immediately tried to rescue her and sent her to a relative's house in Wusong to stay temporarily, while notifying her family to come to Song to take her back.

Arson and Framing Are Extremely Unlawful

Guo Yuanzhong, a native of Gaoyou, leased a piece of vacant land on Limin Road in Hongkou from a landlord six years ago (the lease term was ten years). In addition to building more than ten bungalows and opening a Yunban Wood Factory, he rented out the remaining vacant land to his fellow villagers, Xia Lixi, Li Yongkui, and others, to build thatched sheds to avoid wind and rain. They had always been at peace. Recently, Guo Yuanzhong demanded 50 yuan from Xia Lixi for an old debt, but Xia bore a grudge and thought of a way to retaliate. He secretly instructed others to buy boards from the Yunji Plank Wood Factory on the pretext, and when people were unprepared, they poured kerosene on the boards. Xia and others then claimed that the plank wood factory intended to commit arson to claim insurance money. This was discovered by the police station in charge, and Guo Yuanzhong was immediately arrested and taken to the station. According to Guo's confession, he was actually framed by Xia Lixi, Li Yongkui, and others. Although his factory was insured for a thousand yuan, the planks, houses, and means of livelihood in the factory were worth no less than three or four thousand gold. He was ordered to summon Xia Lixi, Li Yongkui, and Chen Dazhaozi, Xu Taibao, Xu Baocheng, and Li Wangshi, the tenants of the thatched sheds involved, to court. Chen Dazhaozi and others testified that it was indeed Xia Lixi and Li Yongkui who conspired to frame Guo. The day before yesterday, it was ordered that all the people involved be transferred to the Local Court, where Prosecutor Zhang Zi investigated and sentenced Guo Yuanzhong, Xia Lixi, and Li Yongkui to be detained separately, pending further investigation and verification.

A Quarrel Leads to Homicide

Wang Zhen's Death by Clubbing

Wang Tugen, who lives at No. 25 Jinjia Lane in the northern part of Caohejing Town in western Shanghai and runs a teahouse, reported to the Caohejing Police Station at 10:30 p.m. the day before yesterday that a civilian had been eating wedding wine at his maternal uncle Shen Genyu's house nearby today. Madam Zhao, the mother of Hu Xirong, the deputy tax commissioner and former Chinese secretary of the Jianghai Customs, passed away in Shanghai last year on New Year's Eve at the age of 83. Arts and Literature

Establishment of the Wave Literary Society: Amateur young writers Chen Zemin, Chen Chonghua, and others have been dedicated to the folk literary movement. Medical and Pharmaceutical Fields

Li Menghua's Achievements: Li Menghua, a famous doctor in Baichang, is known for his expertise in internal and external medicine, as well as typhoid fever and tuberculosis. The son of Cao Jishi of West Shanghai suffered from a slight hematological disorder for many years, as well as gum disease and nocturnal emission, and his body was getting thinner day by day, gradually reaching the point of no return. Many doctors tried to treat him, but after Mr. Li's careful treatment, taking care of all the diseases, he recovered in less than two months. After Cao's son recovered, he went to Mr. Li's residence at No. 12 Tianyou Lane, Xujiahui, to express his gratitude. He looked energetic and completely different from before.
