Shen Bao Local Supplement Movie Special

Responding to the Needs of the Times Lido Grand Theater Will Be Completed

— Hua

Shanghai is the Paris of the East! It possesses everything that the most modern city of the twentieth century has. Rows of chimneys, bustling carriages, busy people; working all day long, using their brains. Under these circumstances, to obtain a noble form of entertainment in one's spare time, there is simply no more suitable place than a movie theater, and what we urgently need is a theater for first-run movies.

Shanghai is also the New York of the East, a paradise for extravagance, splendor, wealth and wealthy merchants, and a playground for important politicians. Gold is everywhere, and second-run movie theaters seem unnecessary. However, in such a large Shanghai, with more than three million people, how many are wealthy merchants, tycoons, politicians, and important people? They are only a very small number! From this point of view, the audience of first-run movie theaters, in addition to the wealthy, are mostly due to the lack of second-run movie theaters that are suitable for the times, or because the enjoyment they receive is too different from the price they pay. Therefore, the second-run movie theaters that we advocate as urgently needed should have all the equipment of first-run movie theaters, but only charge half the price. So that everyone can have the opportunity to entertain their minds and bodies. We must strive to achieve comfortable equipment and low prices. Now, the Lido Grand Theater, which is about to be completed at the corner of Guizhou Road and Beijing Road, has more luxurious and magnificent equipment than first-run movie theaters.

The construction of the Lido Grand Theater is entirely three-dimensional. All patterns, colors, designs, configurations, and even the patterns on the ground have been carefully considered by experts.

For sound movies, of course, special attention should be paid to the sound. The sound system purchased by Lido is produced by Western Electric Company. Of course, this is the most satisfactory sound system, but in order to guarantee the sound, a huge amount of money was spent to purchase non-combustible, positive sound paperboard Celotex to be inlaid on the walls to absorb sound waves, so that there is no echo problem. Among the movie theaters in this city, only the Great Shanghai and Lido have this equipment. At the same time, Lido's projectors have sufficient non-wiring, except for a few first-run theaters, I am afraid that none can compare to it.

As for the seat equipment, we should pay more attention to it. During the two-hour viewing time, we really don't want to suffer physical pain. The entire Lido theater now uses spring-cushioned seats, and the height and width of the position are all satisfactory to us. In addition to all the luxury and comfort, it charges extremely low prices. With the equipment of a first-run movie theater and only charging half the price, I am afraid that only Lido can do it!

In terms of management, under the management of someone with more than 20 years of movie theater experience, the safety and comfort of the audience can be guaranteed.

Lido is about to open, let's look forward to it!

Movie Review

Review of "Suspicion and Deep Love"

— Warren

Beady for Love Great Light

Due to accidental misunderstandings, rumors spread widely, and then were embellished to form a so-called "public opinion." A lively scene turned into many tragic and comedic stories for the parties involved in confusion. This is very dramatic. Irish female writer Gregory's "City Tiger" (translated as "Rumor") is a famous play made from these materials. However, if the author does not critically focus on the social significance of such events, then no matter how bizarre and interesting the event itself is, and no matter how clever and wonderful the author's technique is, what is created will inevitably be just like this.

"Suspicion and Deep Love" is such an example. It tells the story of a young girl, Mary Ke, who cried because she lost her beloved puppy. People mistakenly thought she was the mistress of a certain libertine who was holding a funeral at the time, so she was disgraced by everyone. Women envied and despised her under the mask of hypocrisy. However, the dance hall manager and theater owners regarded her as a tool to make money and hired her with heavy money.

Now that "yellow news" is especially welcomed by the general public in this turbulent and distressed society, if the playwright can emphatically expose and satirize Mary Ke's unfortunate experience, targeting the "fabricated rape case" and "false lawsuit case" of certain people, it may not be possible to make a meaningful film. However, the playwright only conventionally focused on the love entanglement between Mary Ke and a young reporter, dragging the tail of lovers finally getting married, and vulgarizing the extremely dramatic subject matter.

It is true that it also exposes the fact that the libertine, who was notorious during his lifetime, was given a grand funeral after his death, and celebrities were invited to cover up his shame, and uses satirical techniques to talk about the relationship between father and son, and husband and wife. However, the author did not deal with it with an exposing or satirical attitude, but only touched on it slightly for the development of the play or to add jokes.

From the perspective of performance, director Marion Gering's technique is still light and fast, such as using the soft sound of the milk truck to write out this quiet school dormitory, which cannot contain this active woman. The several appearances of Mary Ke's puppy weight the development of the plot later, but it does not feel tedious. From the instructions of Mary Ke's mother to her on the train, from Mary Ke's charming and lovable attitude in the "basketball meeting" to her shame and resentment when she was tied up and humiliated, she showed her innocence. The change of scenes and tones is quite lively and beautiful. The scene where the young reporter advises Mary Ke to become a dancer, and his quarrel with her mother and managers, is also very lively and powerful. However, the process of Mary Ke feeling empty after losing the reporter Qiu Lin and suddenly realizing it is too fast. I think it would be more effective if she had a successful performance on stage, or if another young man had some love entanglement with her before looking for Qiu Lin again, for the aforementioned Qiu Lin's angry departure.

Ida Lupino played better. Li Qiaolun's personality and physique seem unsuitable for playing the role of a small-town reporter.

Hollywood Anecdotes

— Donglin

It is unbelievable that Shirley Temple would lose 10,000 gold yuan in a week. The fact is this: a broadcasting station in Green Shirt Shore once asked Shirley to broadcast for the station for a reward of 3,500 gold yuan per week; and a theater troupe in New York was willing to hire her to perform on stage for 6,500 gold yuan per week. However, Shirley's parents, fearing that she would become more famous as a result, and that things would become uncontrollable in the future, simply and happily refused for her. That is to say, she lost 10,000 gold yuan in a week!

According to reports, every year, a total of 5,000 girls come to Hollywood, willing to become stars. However, only about two percent of them can truly achieve their goals. The White Byram Stanley couple, seeing this pitiful fact, expressed their sympathy for these girls very much, so in order to help them, they hired thirteen maids!

Ramon Novarro's brother, Antonio Samaniego, recently founded a film company in Mexico. It is said that this Novarro, who has long retired from the film industry, will star in a film. This is truly an expression of brotherly love.

Recently, Gary Cooper's father was injured by a car, and this filial son Gary, I heard, put aside his filming work and sat in the hospital to take care of his father for three consecutive days.

Famous director Frank Capra signed a new three-year contract with MGM again. Hearing this really makes people "brighten their eyes." He always rests for eight months a year! So he only works for four months a year. A money-maker is indeed extraordinary!

Mickey Mouse creator Walt Disney will sue a biscuit company. The reason is that without his permission, the company actually manufactured "Mickey Mouse-shaped" biscuits!

News came that Universal Pictures will set up a production field in Germany specializing in foreign language versions.

This publication is a film publication that assists cultural promotion and art. We welcome all external manuscripts, and the remuneration will be generous once published.

Once a text is published, the copyright belongs to Shen Bao.

This publication's texts are mainly written in colloquial Chinese and must use modern punctuation marks.

When submitting a manuscript, each piece must be stamped, otherwise it will be rejected.

This publication has limited space, so the text should be as short as possible, with each manuscript limited to about 500 words.

Movie Novels

相逢待嫁（Forsaking all Ochers）（三）

— Su Yin

Geoffrey was shocked when he arrived at Manli's house. He stood in the outer room, his back to the signed wall, looking at the hall inside, which was full of guests, men and women, bustling back and forth, talking and laughing. Some were holding champagne glasses and drinking cocktails, some were dancing to the jazz music from the radio, and some were standing idly smoking. Eleanor, dancing, approached Geoffrey, the first to see him. In a moment, Geoffrey became the center of a large group. Everyone asked him questions at once, making him unable to keep up. He looked around, searching for Manli, and Dielun came over. He was delighted to see his old friend after so many years. He could hardly believe that it was really Geoffrey back from abroad. "This is great! This is strange! This place is only missing you… You've really come back!" he said, one after another.

Geoffrey was puzzled and said, "What exactly is going on? What are all these people here for?" Dielun said, "Don't you know yet? What's the matter? Oh… I thought you came specifically for this! This is the greatest evening…" Dielun wanted to ask more, but a girl's voice interrupted his question. That voice was the voice Geoffrey wanted to hear. It was Manli's voice. Manli then ran down the stairs, shouting as she ran! "Where is he? Where is he?"

She stood at the door, as beautiful as a painting. She had already seen Geoffrey, and Geoffrey had already seen her. The two of them looked at each other for a while, as if in a dream, speechless. Later, the two of them met in the center of the hall. Geoffrey hugged her tightly in his arms and kissed her passionately. After a while, Geoffrey pushed Manli away, scrutinizing her, as if somewhat frightened. Manli said, "Geoffrey, darling, you're here, everything is complete, there's nothing wrong…" Geoffrey interrupted, "What do you mean, nothing wrong? Is this a game of hide-and-seek that I have to find myself?" Dielun laughed from the side, "Manli, he doesn't know yet…" Geoffrey… Manli quickly stopped him, saying, "Let me tell him. Geoffrey, I'm going to be Mrs. Dielun Duoda!"

Geoffrey suddenly took a deep breath. In that terrible instant, the world around him seemed to be destroyed, and there were no sun, moon, or stars in the sky. He had come all the way from abroad, originally for Manli. He said for Manli, even if he had to swim back from abroad, he would be willing. But now…" After a while, his senses gradually returned. He forced a smile on his face, but he couldn't speak. Manli kept looking at him, as if searching for something. She said, "Well, aren't you happy? Aren't you congratulating me? Aren't you telling Dielun to take good care of our Nair? Aren't you going to kiss the bride?"

Geoffrey gave a helpless dry laugh, gently pinched Manli's cheek, then turned around and said to Dielun, "Take good care… of… our… Nair…" Everyone laughed. Dielun said loudly, "Our Nair will take care of herself!" Manli grabbed Geoffrey's hand again and said, "You come and give the bride away" (note, this means to be the officiant). Geoffrey nodded slightly. He thought to himself that no matter what, he would never be more heartbroken than he was now. So he said, "Of course, I'll give you away." He paused and added, "Why wouldn't I give you away?" Geoffrey then forced himself to talk to everyone. He also talked privately with Manli for a long time, but he didn't say anything. The taste of sweetness, sourness, bitterness, and spiciness in his heart soon faded away as everyone dispersed. The unmarried male guests all went to attend the bachelor's dinner. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Pictorial Supplement

(1) Italian Ambassador Arrives in China

— (Photographed by Xu Tianzhang)

Following the upgrading of diplomatic envoys between China and Italy, Vincenzo, the first Italian Ambassador to our country, arrived in Shanghai on the Italian ship Conte Rosso on the 7th of this month. The picture shows him disembarking.

(2) The Italian Ambassador and his wife

— (Photographed by Xu Tianzhang)

(3) Zhang Naiyan Returns to China

— (Photographed by Xu Tianzhang)

Zhang Naiyan, our country's envoy to Belgium, was summoned back to China and arrived in Shanghai on the same ship as the Italian Ambassador on the 7th of this month. This is a picture of him disembarking.

(4) All Members of the Zhejiang Provincial Government Take Office

— (Photographed by Wang Yifei)

Huang Shaoxiong, Chairman of Zhejiang Province, and all members of the Provincial Committee took office. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and his wife, and representatives of the Central Government and the National Government, Chu Minyi and Zheng Wenli, all attended the ceremony. The picture shows a group photo in front of the Provincial Government building after the inauguration.

(5) After attending the inauguration ceremony from the lounge, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek asked the person wearing a gown and mandarin jacket, Huang Shaoxiong, the chairman of the province, to wear a military cap. The new adjutant He Yun is standing behind the rockery.

— (Photographed by Wang Yifei)

(6) Madam Song Meiling Chiang Kai-shek, accompanied by Mrs. Huang Shaoxiong and her daughter, attends the inauguration ceremony in the auditorium.

— (Photographed by Wang Yifei)

(7) The National Woodcut Exhibition Opens at the Imperial Ancestral Temple in Beiping

Participating groups included seven units from Guangdong, Shanghai, Zhejiang, Hankou, Pingjin, and Hebei, with over six hundred works. Many visitors attended.

(8) New Year's Day Military Parade

— (Photographed by International News Service)

Chen Guofu, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government and Commander of the Peace Preservation Forces, held a military parade on New Year's Day. The picture shows the Peace Preservation Forces under review passing the commander's platform.

Page 28

(1) Aftermath of the London Naval Conference

The London Naval Conference has ended without result, which was generally expected. From now on, countries will engage in unlimited arms competition, and the crisis of a second world war is drawing closer. The picture shows the representatives of the three countries (from left to right), Standley (US), Simon (UK), and Matsudaira (Japan), and Davis (US) engaging in informal talks after playing golf at the Walton golf course in an attempt to break the deadlock.

(2) Chaco War Situation

The two small South American countries, Paraguay and Bolivia, have been at war over the Grand Chaco dispute for two years. Although the Paraguayan army is currently dominant, Bolivia is mobilizing nationwide to make a last-ditch effort. The final victory is still unknown. The picture shows the Paraguayan army preparing to set off in the war zone.

(3) Bathtub Carved from a Tree Trunk

The bathtubs used by the Paraguayan army in the war zone are carved from tree trunks. The Paraguayan soldiers bathe in them.

(4) Groundbreaking Ceremony for the Fish Market

Chen Gongbo, Minister of the Ministry of Industry, observed the laying of the cornerstone at the groundbreaking ceremony for the Shanghai Fish Market.

(5) Shandong Construction: A plan for seven silt-absorbing field projects is proposed for the sandy land on both sides of the Yellow River. 21-inch siphon pipes will be set up in Licheng Wangjiali, the junction of Qidong Qingcheng, and Mazhazi, each costing 10,000 ocean dollars. 18-inch pipes will be set up in Qihe Hongmiao, costing 7,000 ocean dollars. 15-inch pipes will be set up in Putai Wangwangzhuang, costing 5,000 ocean dollars. All will be completed before the major flood this year. Water is currently being released to silt up the fields. The land near Mazhazi has already dried up, revealing 800 mu of fertile fields with an average silt thickness of one meter. In the past, no crops could grow on this land, but now winter wheat has been sown, and the green seedlings are flourishing everywhere. The picture shows the siphon pipe at Mazhazi drawing water from the Yellow River.

(6) The Shandong Provincial Department of Construction is dredging the Xiaoqing River to allow seagoing vessels under 3,000 tons to reach Yangjiaogou directly, steamships of 600 tons to reach Huangtaiqiao directly, and barges of 200 tons to reach Jinan City and the northern commercial port. The most important completed projects are three: one is the Wuliuzha ship lock and weir project, one is the Bianjiazhuang ship lock and Qishui weir project, and one is the inner river dredging project, which created two bucket dredgers. The picture shows the completed Bianjiazhuang weir.

(7) The Third Drama Performance of the Nanjing Mofeng Art Society

— (Photographed by Xu Chengjie)

A scene from Ibsen's famous work "Nora," with Ms. Chatherine playing Helmer.

(8) Public Writing Problem Office

— (Photographed by Shu Shaonan)

The Hankou Public Education Center has specially set up public writing and inquiry offices at train stations and wharves to write letters for illiterate people and to guide lost travelers. This is the writing and inquiry office at Dazhimen Station.

(9) Famous Ladies on the Beihai Ice Rink in Beiping

— (Photographed by Wei Shouzhong)

From right to left: Ms. Ximeizi, Ms. Chuping, Ms. Yuan.

(10) Ms. Chen Yuxiu, Who Takes the Stage in Opera

— (Photographed by Zhang Zhongshan)

Ms. Chen is the wife of Mr. Shen Shiyi and is skilled in Peking Opera. This is her performance of "Empress He Scolds the Palace" at the Shanghai Lake Society.
